     <div class="feed-shared-inline-show-more-text feed-shared-update-v2__description feed-shared-inline-show-more-text--minimal-padding feed-shared-inline-show-more-text--2-lines" tabindex="-1">
      <div class="update-components-text relative update-components-update-v2__commentary" dir="ltr">
       <!-- -->
       <span class="break-words tvm-parent-container">
        <!-- -->
        <span dir="ltr">
         <!-- -->
         üîç Carve-outs: how to make a success of a key stage in operator transformation?
         <!-- -->
         <span>
          <br/>
         </span>
         <span>
          <br/>
         </span>
         <!-- -->
         In mergers, acquisitions and spin-offs, carve-outs ensure a company's autonomy before integration or sale.
         <!-- -->
         <span>
          <br/>
         </span>
         <span>
          <br/>
         </span>
         <!-- -->
         üìä What's at stake?
         <!-- -->
         <span>
          <br/>
         </span>
         <span class="white-space-pre">
         </span>
         Maintaining operations during restructuring;
         <!-- -->
         <span>
          <br/>
         </span>
         <span class="white-space-pre">
         </span>
         Gaining the trust of stakeholders through clear documentation;
         <!-- -->
         <span>
          <br/>
         </span>
         <span class="white-space-pre">
         </span>
         Managing staff transitions and change management.
         <!-- -->
         <span>
          <br/>
         </span>
         <span>
          <br/>
         </span>
         <!-- -->
         In parallel with the carve-out, we also need to prepare for this transformation, supporting teams and preparing them for change at both ends: in other words, on the side of the entity to be hived off, but also on the side of the parent company.
         <!-- -->
         <span>
          <br/>
         </span>
         <span>
          <br/>
         </span>
         <!-- -->

         </span>

          https://loom.ly/0wmlUxU
          <!-- -->
         </a>
